+package org.forgerock.json.resource.http;
+
+import static org.forgerock.json.resource.QueryResult.*;
+import static org.forgerock.json.resource.http.HttpUtils.*;
+import static org.forgerock.util.Utils.closeSilently;
+
+import javax.mail.internet.ContentType;
+import javax.mail.internet.ParseException;
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.util.List;
+import java.util.Map;
+
+import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.JsonGenerator;
+import org.forgerock.http.Response;
+import org.forgerock.http.ResponseException;
+import org.forgerock.http.header.ContentTypeHeader;
+import org.forgerock.json.fluent.JsonValue;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ActionRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.AdviceContext;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.Connection;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.CreateRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.DeleteRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.PatchRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.QueryRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.QueryResult;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.QueryResultHandler;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ReadRequest;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.Request;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.RequestVisitor;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.Resource;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ResourceException;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ResourceName;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.UpdateRequest;
+import org.forgerock.resource.core.Context;
+import org.forgerock.resource.core.routing.RouterContext;
+import org.forgerock.util.encode.Base64url;
+import org.forgerock.util.promise.AsyncFunction;
+import org.forgerock.util.promise.Promise;
+import org.forgerock.util.promise.Promises;
+
+/**
+ * Common request processing.
+ */
+final class RequestRunner implements RequestVisitor&lt;Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt;, Void&gt; {
+
+    // Connection set on handleResult(Connection).
+    private Connection connection = null;
+    private final Context context;
+    private final org.forgerock.http.Request httpRequest;
+    private final Response httpResponse;
+    private final Request request;
+    private final JsonGenerator writer;
+
+    RequestRunner(Context context, Request request, org.forgerock.http.Request httpRequest, Response httpResponse)
+            throws Exception {
+        this.context = context;
+        this.request = request;
+        this.httpRequest = httpRequest;
+        this.httpResponse = httpResponse;
+        this.writer = getJsonGenerator(httpRequest, httpResponse);
+    }
+
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; handleError(final ResourceException error) {
+        onError(error);
+        return fail(httpRequest, error);
+    }
+
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; handleResult(final Connection result) {
+        connection = result;
+
+        // Dispatch request using visitor.
+        return request.accept(this, null);
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitActionRequest(final Void p, final ActionRequest request) {
+        return connection.actionAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(new AsyncFunction&lt;JsonValue, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(JsonValue result) throws ResponseException {
+                        try {
+                            writeAdvice();
+                            if (result != null) {
+                                writeJsonValue(result);
+                            } else {
+                                // No content.
+                                httpResponse.setStatus(204);
+                            }
+                            onSuccess();
+                        } catch (final Exception e) {
+                            onError(e);
+                        }
+
+                        return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(httpResponse);
+                    }
+                }, new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                        return handleError(e);
+                    }
+                });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitCreateRequest(final Void p, final CreateRequest request) {
+        return connection.createAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(new AsyncFunction&lt;Resource, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(Resource result) throws ResponseException {
+                        try {
+                            writeAdvice();
+                            if (result.getId() != null) {
+                                httpResponse.getHeaders().putSingle(HEADER_LOCATION, getResourceURL(request,
+                                        result));
+                            }
+                            httpResponse.setStatus(201);
+                            writeResource(result);
+                            onSuccess();
+                        } catch (final Exception e) {
+                            onError(e);
+                        }
+                        return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(httpResponse);
+                    }
+                }, new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                        return handleError(e);
+                    }
+                });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitDeleteRequest(final Void p, final DeleteRequest request) {
+        return connection.deleteAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(newResourceSuccessHandler(),
+                        new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                            @Override
+                            public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                                return handleError(e);
+                            }
+                        });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitPatchRequest(final Void p, final PatchRequest request) {
+        return connection.patchAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(newResourceSuccessHandler(),
+                        new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                            @Override
+                            public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                                return handleError(e);
+                            }
+                        });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitQueryRequest(final Void p, final QueryRequest request) {
+        return connection.queryAsync(context, request, new QueryResultHandler() {
+            private boolean isFirstResult = true;
+            private int resultCount = 0;
+
+            @Override
+            public void handleError(final ResourceException error) {
+                if (isFirstResult) {
+                    onError(error);
+                } else {
+                    // Partial results - it's too late to set the status.
+                    try {
+                        writer.writeEndArray();
+                        writer.writeNumberField(FIELD_RESULT_COUNT, resultCount);
+                        writer.writeObjectField(FIELD_ERROR, error.toJsonValue().getObject());
+                        writer.writeEndObject();
+                        onSuccess();
+                    } catch (final Exception e) {
+                        onError(e);
+                    }
+                }
+            }
+
+            @Override
+            public boolean handleResource(final Resource resource) {
+                try {
+                    writeAdvice();
+                    writeHeader();
+                    writeJsonValue(resource.getContent());
+                    resultCount++;
+                    return true;
+                } catch (final Exception e) {
+                    handleError(adapt(e));
+                    return false;
+                }
+            }
+
+            @Override
+            public void handleResult(final QueryResult result) {
+                try {
+                    writeHeader();
+                    writer.writeEndArray();
+                    writer.writeNumberField(FIELD_RESULT_COUNT, resultCount);
+                    writer.writeStringField(FIELD_PAGED_RESULTS_COOKIE, result
+                            .getPagedResultsCookie());
+                    writer.writeNumberField(FIELD_REMAINING_PAGED_RESULTS, result
+                            .getRemainingPagedResults());
+                    writer.writeEndObject();
+                    onSuccess();
+                } catch (final Exception e) {
+                    onError(e);
+                }
+            }
+
+            private void writeHeader() throws IOException {
+                if (isFirstResult) {
+                    writer.writeStartObject();
+                    writer.writeArrayFieldStart(FIELD_RESULT);
+                    isFirstResult = false;
+                }
+            }
+        })
+                .thenAsync(new AsyncFunction&lt;QueryResult, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(QueryResult queryResult) throws ResponseException {
+                        return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(httpResponse);
+                    }
+                }, new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                    @Override
+                    public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                        return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(httpResponse);
+                    }
+                });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitReadRequest(final Void p, final ReadRequest request) {
+        return connection.readAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(newResourceSuccessHandler(),
+                        new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                            @Override
+                            public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                                return handleError(e);
+                            }
+                        });
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * {@inheritDoc}
+     */
+    @Override
+    public final Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; visitUpdateRequest(final Void p, final UpdateRequest request) {
+        return connection.updateAsync(context, request)
+                .thenAsync(newResourceSuccessHandler(),
+                        new AsyncFunction&lt;ResourceException, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+                            @Override
+                            public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(ResourceException e) throws ResponseException {
+                                return handleError(e);
+                            }
+                        });
+    }
+
+    private void onSuccess() {
+        closeSilently(connection, writer);
+    }
+
+    private void onError(final Exception e) {
+        // Don't close the JSON writer because the request will become
+        // &quot;completed&quot; which then prevents us from sending an error.
+        closeSilently(connection);
+    }
+
+    private String getResourceURL(final CreateRequest request, final Resource resource) {
+        // Strip out everything except the scheme and host.
+        StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder()
+                .append(httpRequest.getUri().getScheme())
+                .append(&quot;://&quot;)
+                .append(httpRequest.getUri().getRawAuthority());
+
+        // Add back the context path.
+        builder.append(context.asContext(RouterContext.class).getMatchedUri());
+
+        // Add new resource name and resource ID.
+        final ResourceName resourceName = request.getResourceNameObject();
+        if (!resourceName.isEmpty()) {
+            builder.append('/');
+            builder.append(resourceName);
+        }
+        builder.append('/');
+        builder.append(resource.getId());
+
+        return builder.toString();
+    }
+
+    private AsyncFunction&lt;Resource, Response, ResponseException&gt; newResourceSuccessHandler() {
+        return new AsyncFunction&lt;Resource, Response, ResponseException&gt;() {
+            @Override
+            public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; apply(Resource result) {
+                try {
+                    writeAdvice();
+                    // Don't return the resource if this is a read request and the
+                    // If-None-Match header was specified.
+                    if (request instanceof ReadRequest) {
+                        final String rev = getIfNoneMatch(httpRequest);
+                        if (rev != null &amp;&amp; rev.equals(result.getRevision())) {
+                            // No change so 304.
+                            Map&lt;String, Object&gt; responseBody = ResourceException.getException(304)
+                                    .setReason(&quot;Not Modified&quot;).toJsonValue().asMap();
+                            return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(new Response().setStatusAndReason(304)
+                                    .setEntity(responseBody));
+                        }
+                    }
+                    writeResource(result);
+                    onSuccess();
+                } catch (final Exception e) {
+                    onError(e);
+                }
+                return Promises.newSuccessfulPromise(httpResponse);
+            }
+        };
+    }
+
+    private void writeJsonValue(final JsonValue json) throws IOException {
+        writer.writeObject(json.getObject());
+    }
+
+    private void writeTextValue(final JsonValue json) throws IOException {
+        if (json.isMap() &amp;&amp; !json.asMap().isEmpty()) {
+            writeToResponse(json.asMap().entrySet().iterator().next().getValue().toString().getBytes());
+        } else if (json.isList() &amp;&amp; !json.asList().isEmpty()) {
+            writeToResponse(json.asList(String.class).iterator().next().getBytes());
+        } else if (json.isString()) {
+            writeToResponse(json.asString().getBytes());
+        } else if (json.isBoolean()) {
+            writeToResponse(json.asBoolean().toString().getBytes());
+        } else if (json.isNumber()) {
+            writeToResponse(json.asNumber().toString().getBytes());
+        } else {
+            throw new IOException(&quot;Content is unknown type or is empty&quot;);
+        }
+    }
+
+    private void writeBinaryValue(final JsonValue json) throws IOException {
+        if (json.isMap() &amp;&amp; !json.asMap().isEmpty()) {
+            writeToResponse(Base64url.decode(json.asMap().entrySet().iterator().next().getValue().toString()));
+        } else if (json.isList() &amp;&amp; !json.asList().isEmpty()) {
+            writeToResponse(Base64url.decode(json.asList(String.class).iterator().next()));
+        } else if (json.isString()) {
+            writeToResponse(Base64url.decode(json.asString()));
+        } else {
+            throw new IOException(&quot;Content is not an accepted type or is empty&quot;);
+        }
+    }
+
+    private void writeToResponse(byte[] data) throws IOException {
+        if (data == null || data.length == 0) {
+            throw new IOException(&quot;Content is empty or corrupt&quot;);
+        }
+        httpResponse.setEntity(data);
+    }
+
+    private void writeResource(final Resource resource) throws IOException, ParseException {
+        if (resource.getRevision() != null) {
+            final StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder();
+            builder.append('&quot;');
+            builder.append(resource.getRevision());
+            builder.append('&quot;');
+            httpResponse.getHeaders().putSingle(HEADER_ETAG, builder.toString());
+        }
+
+        ContentType contentType = new ContentType(ContentTypeHeader.valueOf(httpResponse).toString());
+
+        if (contentType.match(MIME_TYPE_APPLICATION_JSON)) {
+            writeJsonValue(resource.getContent());
+        } else if (contentType.match(MIME_TYPE_TEXT_PLAIN)) {
+            writeTextValue(resource.getContent());
+        } else {
+            writeBinaryValue(resource.getContent());
+        }
+    }
+
+    private void writeAdvice() {
+        if (context.containsContext(AdviceContext.class)) {
+            AdviceContext adviceContext = context.asContext(AdviceContext.class);
+            for (Map.Entry&lt;String, List&lt;String&gt;&gt; entry : adviceContext.getAdvices().entrySet()) {
+                httpResponse.getHeaders().put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
+            }
+        }
+    }
+}
</ins></span></pre></div>

</span><ins>+/*

+ * Header, with the fields enclosed by brackets [] replaced by your own identifying
+ * information: &quot;Portions copyright [year] [name of copyright owner]&quot;.
+ *
+ * Copyright 2012-2014 ForgeRock AS.
+ */
+
+package org.forgerock.json.resource.http;
+
+import java.util.Map;
+
+import org.forgerock.http.HttpContext;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.InternalServerErrorException;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ResourceException;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.SecurityContext;
+import org.forgerock.resource.core.Context;
+
+/**
+ * An HTTP context factory which will create a {@link SecurityContext} whose
+ * authentication ID and authorization ID are taken from attributes contained
+ * in the HTTP request.
+ * &lt;p&gt;
+ * This class provides integration with the common authentication framework and
+ * is intended to work as follows:
+ * &lt;ol&gt;
+ * &lt;li&gt;An incoming HTTP request is first intercepted by a HTTP filter
+ * responsible for authenticating the request.
+ * &lt;li&gt;If authentication is successful, the authentication filter determines the
+ * set of principals associated with the user which may be required in order to
+ * perform authorization. These principals may include the user's unique ID,
+ * realm, groups, roles, or LDAP DN, etc.
+ * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter constructs a {@code Map&lt;String, Object&gt;}
+ * containing the principals keyed on the principal name. &lt;b&gt;NOTE:&lt;/b&gt; various
+ * reserved principal names are defined in {@link SecurityContext}.
+ * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter stores the authentication ID (the name which
+ * the user identified themselves with during authentication) in the HTTP
+ * servlet request's {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute.
+ * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter stores the {@code Map} containing the
+ * authorization principals in the HTTP servlet request's
+ * {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID} attribute.
+ * &lt;li&gt;The JSON Resource Handler uses the {@code SecurityContextFactory} to
+ * obtain the authentication ID and authorization principals from the HTTP
+ * request's attributes.
+ * &lt;/ol&gt;
+ * The following code illustrates how an authentication HTTP filter can
+ * populate the attributes:
+ *
+ * &lt;pre&gt;
+ * public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; (Context context, org.forgerock.http.Request request, Handler next) {
+ *     // Authenticate the user.
+ *     String authcid = getUserName(request);
+ *     String password = getPassword(request);
+ *
+ *     // Add the attributes.
+ *     if (checkCredentials(authcid, password)) {
+ *         // Obtain principals for authorization.
+ *         Map&lt;String, Object&gt; authzid = new HashMap&lt;String, Object&gt;();
+ *         authzid.put(AUTHZID_ID, id);
+ *         ...
+ *
+ *         org.forgerock.http.HttpContext httpContext = context.asContext(org.forgerock.http.HttpContext.class);
+ *         httpContext.getAttributes().put(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID, authcid);
+ *         httpContext.getAttributes().put(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID, authzid);
+ *     }
+ * }
+ * &lt;/pre&gt;
+ */
+public final class SecurityContextFactory implements HttpContextFactory {
+
+    /**
+     * The name of the HTTP Request attribute where this factory expects to
+     * find the authenticated user's authentication ID. The name of this
+     * attribute is {@code org.forgerock.authentication.principal} and it MUST
+     * contain a {@code String} if it is present.
+     *
+     * @see SecurityContext#getAuthenticationId()
+     */
+    public static final String ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID = &quot;org.forgerock.authentication.principal&quot;;
+
+    /**
+     * The name of the HTTP Request attribute where this factory expects to
+     * find the authenticated user's authorization ID. The name of this
+     * attribute is {@code org.forgerock.authentication.context} and it MUST
+     * contain a {@code Map&lt;String, Object&gt;} if it is present.
+     *
+     * @see SecurityContext#getAuthorizationId()
+     */
+    public static final String ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID = &quot;org.forgerock.authentication.context&quot;;
+
+    // Singleton instance.
+    private static final SecurityContextFactory INSTANCE = new SecurityContextFactory();
+
+    /**
+     * Returns the singleton security context factory which can be used for
+     * obtaining context information from a HTTP request.
+     *
+     * @return The singleton security context factory.
+     */
+    public static SecurityContextFactory getHttpServletContextFactory() {
+        return INSTANCE;
+    }
+
+    private SecurityContextFactory() {
+        // Prevent instantiation.
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * Creates a new {@code SecurityContext} using the attributes contained in
+     * the provided HTTP request. The authentication ID will be obtained from
+     * the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute, and the authorization ID will
+     * be obtained from the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute.
+     * &lt;p&gt;
+     * It is not an error if either of the attributes are not present, but a
+     * {@link ResourceException} will be thrown if they are present but have the
+     * wrong type.
+     *
+     * @param parent
+     *            The parent context.
+     * @return A security context initialized using the attributes contained in
+     *         the provided HTTP request.
+     * @throws ResourceException
+     *             If one of the attributes was present but had the wrong type.
+     */
+    public SecurityContext createContext(Context parent) throws ResourceException {
+        HttpContext httpContext = parent.asContext(HttpContext.class);
+        String authcid = getAuthenticationIdAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID, httpContext);
+        Map&lt;String, Object&gt; authzid = getAuthorizationIdAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID, httpContext);
+        return new SecurityContext(parent, authcid, authzid);
+    }
+
+    private String getAuthenticationIdAttribute(String attributeName, org.forgerock.http.HttpContext context)
+            throws InternalServerErrorException {
+        try {
+            return (String) context.getAttributes().get(attributeName);
+        } catch (final ClassCastException e) {
+            throw new InternalServerErrorException(
+                    &quot;The security context could not be created because the &quot;
+                            + &quot;authentication ID attribute, &quot; + attributeName
+                            + &quot;, contained in the HTTP request did not have &quot;
+                            + &quot;the correct type&quot;, e);
+        }
+    }
+
+    @SuppressWarnings(&quot;unchecked&quot;)
+    private Map&lt;String, Object&gt; getAuthorizationIdAttribute(String attributeName,
+            org.forgerock.http.HttpContext context) throws InternalServerErrorException {
+        try {
+            return (Map&lt;String, Object&gt;) context.getAttributes().get(attributeName);
+        } catch (final ClassCastException e) {
+            throw new InternalServerErrorException(
+                    &quot;The security context could not be created because the &quot;
+                            + &quot;authorization ID attribute, &quot; + attributeName
+                            + &quot;, contained in the HTTP request did not have &quot;
+                            + &quot;the correct type&quot;, e);
+        }
+    }
+
+    /**
+     * Creates a new {@code SecurityContext} using the attributes contained in
+     * the provided HTTP request. The authentication ID will be obtained from
+     * the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute, and the authorization ID will
+     * be obtained from the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute.
+     * &lt;p&gt;
+     * It is not an error if either of the attributes are not present, but a
+     * {@link ResourceException} will be thrown if they are present but have the
+     * wrong type.
+     *
+     * @param request
+     *            The HTTP request from which the authentication ID and
+     *            authorization ID attributes should be obtained.
+     * @return A security context initialized using the attributes contained in
+     *         the provided HTTP request.
+     * @throws ResourceException
+     *             If one of the attributes was present but had the wrong type.
+     */
+    @Override
+    public SecurityContext createContext(Context context, org.forgerock.http.Request request)
+            throws ResourceException {
+        return createContext(context);
+    }
+
+}
</ins></span></pre></div>

</span><ins>+&lt;?xml version=&quot;1.0&quot; encoding=&quot;UTF-8&quot;?&gt;
+&lt;!--

+  ! enclosed by brackets &quot;[]&quot; replaced with your own identifying information:
+  !      Portions Copyright [yyyy] [name of copyright owner]
+  !
+  ! CCPL HEADER END
+  !

+  !    
+--&gt;
+&lt;document xmlns=&quot;http://maven.apache.org/XDOC/2.0&quot; xmlns:xsi=&quot;http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance&quot;
+  xsi:schemaLocation=&quot;http://maven.apache.org/XDOC/2.0 http://maven.apache.org/xsd/xdoc-2.0.xsd&quot;&gt;
+  &lt;properties&gt;
+    &lt;title&gt;About ${project.name}&lt;/title&gt;
+    &lt;author&gt;ForgeRock AS&lt;/author&gt;
+  &lt;/properties&gt;
+    &lt;body&gt;
+        &lt;section name=&quot;About ${project.name}&quot;&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                JSON Resource Servlet provides J2EE 6 Servlet integration and
+                defines a common HTTP based REST API for interacting with JSON
+                Resources.
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                The module provides a standalone &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServlet.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServlet&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
+                implementation as part of its WAR artifact. The Servlet can
+                be deployed and configured with a custom
+                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/ConnectionFactory.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;ConnectionFactory&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
+                and &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServletContextFactory.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServletContextFactory&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.
+                By default the Servlet will use an in memory back-end exposing a
+                &quot;/users&quot; and a &quot;/groups&quot; end-point.
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                In addition, the module provides a JAR artifact which can be
+                used for building more complex JSON Resource Servlets. As well
+                as extending the &lt;tt&gt;HttpServlet&lt;/tt&gt; implementation you can
+                also use the &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServletAdapter.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServletAdapter&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
+                which adapts Servlet calls to JSON resource calls. An adapter
+                can be used in any Servlet, just create a new instance and
+                override the &lt;tt&gt;service()&lt;/tt&gt; method in your Servlet to delegate all
+                those calls to the adapter's &lt;tt&gt;service()&lt;/tt&gt; method.
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+        &lt;/section&gt;
+        &lt;section name=&quot;Get ${project.name}&quot;&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                JSON Resource Servlet is built and made available using Maven.
+                Your project can use JSON Resource by declaring the
+                following Maven dependencies:
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;source&gt;&amp;lt;repositories&gt;
+    &amp;lt;repository&gt;
+        &amp;lt;id&gt;forgerock-staging-repository&amp;lt;/id&gt;
+        &amp;lt;name&gt;ForgeRock Release Repository&amp;lt;/name&gt;
+        &amp;lt;url&gt;http://maven.forgerock.org/repo/releases&amp;lt;/url&gt;
+        &amp;lt;snapshots&gt;
+            &amp;lt;enabled&gt;false&amp;lt;/enabled&gt;
+        &amp;lt;/snapshots&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/repository&gt;
+    &amp;lt;repository&gt;
+        &amp;lt;id&gt;forgerock-snapshots-repository&amp;lt;/id&gt;
+        &amp;lt;name&gt;ForgeRock Snapshot Repository&amp;lt;/name&gt;
+        &amp;lt;url&gt;http://maven.forgerock.org/repo/snapshots&amp;lt;/url&gt;
+        &amp;lt;releases&gt;
+            &amp;lt;enabled&gt;false&amp;lt;/enabled&gt;
+        &amp;lt;/releases&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/repository&gt;
+&amp;lt;/repositories&gt;
+
+...
+
+&amp;lt;dependencies&gt;
+    &amp;lt;dependency&gt;
+        &amp;lt;groupId&gt;${project.groupId}&amp;lt;/groupId&gt;
+        &amp;lt;artifactId&gt;json-resource&amp;lt;/artifactId&gt;
+        &amp;lt;version&gt;${project.version}&amp;lt;/version&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/dependency&gt;
+    &amp;lt;dependency&gt;
+        &amp;lt;groupId&gt;${project.groupId}&amp;lt;/groupId&gt;
+        &amp;lt;artifactId&gt;${project.artifactId}&amp;lt;/artifactId&gt;
+        &amp;lt;version&gt;${project.version}&amp;lt;/version&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/dependency&gt;
+&amp;lt;/dependencies&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                See the documentation for
+                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/index.html&quot;&gt;json-resource&lt;/a&gt;
+                for instructions on building your own JSON Resources.
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+        &lt;/section&gt;
+        &lt;section name=&quot;Getting started&quot;&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                The simplest way to get started is to deploy the WAR and
+                configure its &lt;tt&gt;web.xml&lt;/tt&gt; configuration file as needed. By
+                default it has the following key properties:
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;source&gt;&amp;lt;servlet&gt;
+    &amp;lt;servlet-name&gt;Users&amp;lt;/servlet-name&gt;
+    &amp;lt;servlet-class&gt;org.forgerock.json.resource.servlet.HttpServlet&amp;lt;/servlet-class&gt;
+
+    &amp;lt;init-param&gt;
+        &amp;lt;param-name&gt;connection-factory-class&amp;lt;/param-name&gt;
+        &amp;lt;param-value&gt;org.forgerock.json.resource.servlet.MemoryBackendConnectionFactoryProvider&amp;lt;/param-value&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/init-param&gt;
+
+    &amp;lt;init-param&gt;
+        &amp;lt;param-name&gt;uri-template&amp;lt;/param-name&gt;
+        &amp;lt;param-value&gt;&amp;lt;/param-value&gt;
+    &amp;lt;/init-param&gt;
+&amp;lt;/servlet&gt;
+
+&amp;lt;servlet-mapping&gt;
+    &amp;lt;servlet-name&gt;Users&amp;lt;/servlet-name&gt;
+    &amp;lt;url-pattern&gt;/users/*&amp;lt;/url-pattern&gt;
+&amp;lt;/servlet-mapping&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                You can even check out the source code for this Maven module
+                and run the default Servlet directly as follows: 
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;source&gt;mvn jetty:run&lt;/source&gt;
+        &lt;/section&gt;
+        &lt;section name=&quot;Overview of the REST API&quot;&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                JSON Resource Servlet is a library and as such provides a common
+                framework for developing ForgeRock REST APIs. It does not expose
+                any end-points itself, e.g. &lt;tt&gt;users&lt;/tt&gt;, apart from the
+                example Servlet configuration. More specifically, this library
+                defines the types of operations and their parameters, but it
+                is left to the application to define the following:
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;ul&gt;
+                &lt;li&gt;
+                    The end-points - top-level end-points may be defined in the
+                    Servlet configuration using the &lt;tt&gt;servlet-mapping&lt;/tt&gt;
+                    properties, or they may be defined using a
+                    &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/Router.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;Router&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.
+                &lt;/li&gt;
+                &lt;li&gt;
+                    The schema used for resources passed to and from the JSON
+                    Resources. At some point we do expect to define a common
+                    schema for common types of resource, such as users and
+                    groups.
+                &lt;/li&gt;
+                &lt;li&gt;
+                    The set of extended &quot;actions&quot; which may be performed against
+                    a resource. Only the core operations of &quot;create&quot;, &quot;delete&quot;,
+                    &quot;patch&quot;, &quot;query&quot;, &quot;read&quot;, and &quot;update&quot; are specified.
+                &lt;/li&gt;                     
+            &lt;/ul&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                The following sub-sections describe each of the core operations
+                in more detail:
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Creating resources using POST&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    A POST create request should be used when the resource to be
+                    created will have a server provided resource ID (e.g. a
+                    UUID). It may also be used in cases where the resource ID
+                    is client provided, but only as long as the resource ID is
+                    included as a field within the new resource.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    POST create requests should target the resource container
+                    and must include the parameter &lt;tt&gt;_action=create&lt;/tt&gt;.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;POST&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_action=create&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Mandatory parameter which must be equal
+                                to the value &quot;create&quot; indicating that this is a
+                                request to create a new resource.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be created.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was created.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;POST /users?_action=create  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json
+Content-Type: application/json
+Content-Length: ...
+{
+  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
+  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
+}&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Creating resources using PUT&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    A PUT create request should be used when the resource to be
+                    created has a known resource ID. The resource ID is 
+                    specified as part of the target resource name, and may also
+                    be included as a field within the new resource, in which
+                    case the two must be equivalent.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    PUT create requests should target the new resource and
+                    include the HTTP header &lt;tt&gt;If-None-Match: *&lt;/tt&gt;.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;PUT&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be created.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was created.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;PUT /users/1  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json
+Content-Type: application/json
+Content-Length: ...
+If-None-Match: *
+{
+  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
+  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
+}&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Reading resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    To read an existing resource send a GET request targeting
+                    the resource to be read.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;GET&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType=&lt;i&gt;mimeType&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;A string that identifies the media type for the response content.
+                            When this parameter is used only 1 field value may be returned using the &lt;tt&gt;_fields&lt;/tt&gt;
+                            parameter.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was read if the &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType&lt;/tt&gt; parameter
+                            is not used. Otherwise the requested resource field is returned with the content type specified in the
+                                &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType&lt;/tt&gt; parameter&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;GET /users/1  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Querying/listing resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    To search or list the resources contained within a resource
+                    container send a GET request targeting the resource
+                    container and including either a &lt;tt&gt;_queryId&lt;/tt&gt; or
+                    &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter&lt;/tt&gt; parameter.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;GET&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryId=&lt;i&gt;ID&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;A string identifying a server side &quot;stored&quot; query.
+                            This parameter is mandatory if &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter&lt;/tt&gt;
+                            is not specified.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter=&lt;i&gt;FILTER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;A filter expression which will be used to determine
+                            whether or not a resource should be included in the
+                            returned results. The filter format is described in the
+                            Javadoc for the &lt;a
+                            href=&quot;http://commons.forgerock.org/forgerock-rest/json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/QueryFilter.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;QueryFilter&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
+                            class. This parameter is mandatory if
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryId&lt;/tt&gt; is not specified.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_sortKeys=&lt;i&gt;[+-]FIELD,...&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;Optional parameter containing a comma separated
+                            list of field references specifying which fields
+                            of the targeted JSON resources should be used as
+                            sort keys. A sort key is a JSON pointer optionally
+                            prefixed with a &quot;+&quot; or &quot;-&quot; character indicating
+                            whether the key is to be sorted in ascending or
+                            descending order. Default is to not sort results.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_pagedResultsCookie=&lt;i&gt;STRING&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Optional opaque cookie which is used by the
+                                server to track its position in the
+                                set of query results. Paged results will be
+                                enabled if and only if the &lt;tt&gt;_pageSize&lt;/tt&gt; is
+                                non-zero.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                The cookie must be not be specified in the
+                                initial query request. Subsequent query
+                                requests must include the cookie returned with
+                                the previous query result
+                                &lt;tt&gt;pagedResultsCookie&lt;/tt&gt; field, until the
+                                server returns a &lt;tt&gt;null&lt;/tt&gt; cookie indicating
+                                that the final page of results has been returned.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Default behavior is to not return paged query
+                                results.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_pagedResultsOffset=&lt;i&gt;INTEGER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Optional parameter specifying the index within
+                                the result set of the first result which should
+                                be returned. Paged results will be enabled if
+                                and only if the page size is non-zero. If the
+                                parameter is not present or a value less than 1
+                                is specified then the page following the last
+                                page returned will be returned. A value equal
+                                to or greater than 1 indicates that a specific
+                                page should be returned starting from the position
+                                specified.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Default behavior is to return the page following the
+                                previous returned page.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_pageSize=&lt;i&gt;INTEGER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Optional parameter indicating that query results are
+                                returned in pages of the specified size. For all
+                                paged result requests other than the initial
+                                request, a cookie should be provided with the query
+                                request.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Default behavior is to not return paged
+                                query results.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;&lt;i&gt;arg1&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value1&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;arg2&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value2&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;...&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;argn&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;valuen&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;Additional parameters supported by the stored query.
+                            By convention argument names should not begin with
+                            an underscore. It is an error to include additional
+                            parameters if a &lt;tt&gt;_filter&lt;/tt&gt; is specified.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                A JSON object containing the following three fields:
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;ul&gt;
+                                &lt;li&gt;
+                                    &lt;b&gt;results&lt;/b&gt; - an array containing the
+                                    matching resources, or next page of matching
+                                    resources if paged results have been
+                                    requested.
+                                &lt;/li&gt;
+                                &lt;li&gt;
+                                    &lt;b&gt;pagedResultsCookie&lt;/b&gt; - the opaque
+                                    cookie which should be included with the
+                                    next paged results query if paged results
+                                    have been requested, otherwise &lt;tt&gt;null&lt;/tt&gt;. 
+                                &lt;/li&gt;
+                                &lt;li&gt;
+                                    &lt;b&gt;remainingPagedResults&lt;/b&gt; - an estimate
+                                    of the number of remaining paged results, or
+                                    &lt;tt&gt;-1&lt;/tt&gt; if the number is not known, or
+                                    if paged results have not been requested.
+                                &lt;/li&gt;
+                            &lt;/ul&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;GET /users?_queryId=all  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Updating resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    To replace the contents of an existing resource send a PUT
+                    request targeting the new resource and optionally include
+                    the HTTP header &quot;If-Match&quot; specifying the version if
+                    MVCC is needed.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;tt&gt;PUT&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be
+                            updated.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was
+                            updated.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;PUT /users/1  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json
+Content-Type: application/json
+Content-Length: ...
+If-Match: &quot;1&quot;
+{
+  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
+  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
+}&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Patching resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Patch operations are not yet supported.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Deleting resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    To delete an existing resource send a DELETE request targeting
+                    the resource to be deleted and optionally include
+                    the HTTP header &quot;If-Match&quot; specifying the version if
+                    MVCC is needed.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;DELETE&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was deleted.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;DELETE /users/1  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json
+If-Match: &quot;1&quot;&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Performing extended actions against resources&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Some resources may support additional operations which can
+                    performed against them. These operations are performed by
+                    sending a POST request specifying the type of action to be
+                    performed using the &lt;tt&gt;_action&lt;/tt&gt; parameter. The
+                    request may include zero or more implementation specific
+                    parameters.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Note that the action identifier &quot;create&quot; is reserved
+                    exclusively for resource creation.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;POST&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_action=&lt;i&gt;ID&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;Mandatory parameter which identifying the type of
+                            action to be performed against the resource.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;&lt;i&gt;arg1&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value1&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;arg2&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value2&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;...&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;argn&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;valuen&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;Additional parameters supported by the action. By
+                            convention argument names should not begin with an
+                            underscore.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The action specified JSON request content if
+                            applicable.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;The action specified JSON response content if
+                            applicable.&lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    Example:
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;source&gt;POST /tasks/1?_action=cancel  HTTP/1.1
+Host: example.com
+Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Common request parameters&quot;&gt;
+                &lt;p&gt;
+                    The following table lists the common HTTP request parameters
+                    which may be used with any type of request.
+                &lt;/p&gt;
+                &lt;table&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
+                        &lt;th&gt;Description&lt;/th&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_fields=FIELD,...&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Optional parameter containing a comma separated
+                                list of field references specifying which fields
+                                of the targeted JSON resource should be returned.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Default is to return all fields.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                    &lt;tr&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;tt&gt;_prettyPrint=true|false&lt;/tt&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                        &lt;td&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Optional parameter requesting that the returned
+                                JSON resource content should be formatted to be
+                                more human readable.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                            &lt;p&gt;
+                                Default is false.
+                            &lt;/p&gt;
+                        &lt;/td&gt;
+                    &lt;/tr&gt;
+                &lt;/table&gt;
+            &lt;/subsection&gt;
+        &lt;/section&gt;
+        &lt;section name=&quot;Known Issues&quot;&gt;
+            &lt;p&gt;
+                See the documentation for
+                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/index.html&quot;&gt;json-resource&lt;/a&gt;
+                for a list of known issues.
+            &lt;/p&gt;
+        &lt;/section&gt;
+    &lt;/body&gt;
+&lt;/document&gt;
</ins></span></pre></div>

+package org.forgerock.json.resource.http;
+
+import static org.assertj.core.api.Assertions.assertThat;
+import static org.assertj.core.data.MapEntry.entry;
+import static org.forgerock.http.test.HttpTest.newRequest;
+
+import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.io.PrintStream;
+import java.net.URISyntaxException;
+import java.util.Collections;
+import java.util.List;
+
+import org.forgerock.http.Response;
+import org.forgerock.http.header.ContentTypeHeader;
+import org.forgerock.json.fluent.JsonValue;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.BadRequestException;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.PatchOperation;
+import org.forgerock.json.resource.ResourceException;
+import org.forgerock.util.encode.Base64url;
+import org.testng.annotations.BeforeClass;
+import org.testng.annotations.DataProvider;
+import org.testng.annotations.Test;
+
+@SuppressWarnings(&quot;javadoc&quot;)
+public class HttpUtilsTest {
+    private static final String JPEG_PART_NAME = &quot;profile&quot;;
+    private static final String JPEG_PART_FILENAME = &quot;file.jpg&quot;;
+    private static final String JPEG_CONTENT = &quot;This is Jpeg Content&quot;;
+
+    private static final String PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY = &quot;profileFilename&quot;;
+    private static final String PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY = &quot;profileContent&quot;;
+    private static final String PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY = &quot;profileMimeType&quot;;
+    private static final String UID = &quot;uid&quot;;
+    private static final String ALICE = &quot;alice&quot;;
+
+    private static final String JPEG_CONTENT_TYPE = &quot;image/jpeg&quot;;
+
+    private static final String REQUEST_CONTENT_TYPE =
+            &quot;multipart/form-data; boundary=kwkIqb-fsdbtcNpB4dJ_Xqf1-3b0Hp_VF9D0vsgL&quot;;
+
+    private org.forgerock.http.Request request;
+
+    private byte[] requestInputStreamData;
+
+    private String jsonBody;
+    private String jsonPatchBody;
+
+    @BeforeClass
+    public void onTimeSetup() {
+        StringBuilder jsonBody = new StringBuilder();
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;{&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;\&quot;uid\&quot; : \&quot;alice\&quot;,&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;\&quot;email\&quot; : \&quot;alice@example.com\&quot;,&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(
+                &quot;\&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY + &quot;\&quot; : { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME
+                        + &quot;#content\&quot; },&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(
+                &quot;\&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY + &quot;\&quot; : { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME
+                        + &quot;#mimetype\&quot; },&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(
+                &quot;\&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY + &quot;\&quot; : { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME
+                        + &quot;#filename\&quot; }&quot;).append(&quot;\n&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;}&quot;);
+        this.jsonBody = jsonBody.toString();
+
+        jsonBody = new StringBuilder();
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;[&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;{ \&quot;operation\&quot;: \&quot;replace\&quot;, \&quot;field\&quot;: \&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY
+                + &quot;\&quot;, \&quot;value\&quot;: { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#mimetype\&quot; } },&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;{ \&quot;operation\&quot;: \&quot;replace\&quot;, \&quot;field\&quot;: \&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY
+                + &quot;\&quot;, \&quot;value\&quot;: { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#content\&quot; } },&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;{ \&quot;operation\&quot;: \&quot;replace\&quot;, \&quot;field\&quot;: \&quot;&quot; + PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY
+                + &quot;\&quot;, \&quot;value\&quot;: { \&quot;$ref\&quot; : \&quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#filename\&quot; } }&quot;);
+        jsonBody.append(&quot;]&quot;);
+        this.jsonPatchBody = jsonBody.toString();
+    }
+
+    private void createMultiPartRequest(String jsonBody) {
+        ByteArrayOutputStream requestInputStreamData = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
+
+        PrintStream reguestInputStreamData = new PrintStream(requestInputStreamData);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Type: &quot; + REQUEST_CONTENT_TYPE);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println();
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;--kwkIqb-fsdbtcNpB4dJ_Xqf1-3b0Hp_VF9D0vsgL&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Disposition: form-data; name=\&quot;json\&quot;&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Type: application/json; charset=US-ASCII&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Transfer-Encoding: 8bit&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println();
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(jsonBody);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;--kwkIqb-fsdbtcNpB4dJ_Xqf1-3b0Hp_VF9D0vsgL&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Disposition: form-data; name=\&quot;&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME
+                + &quot;\&quot;; filename=\&quot;&quot; + JPEG_PART_FILENAME + &quot;\&quot;&quot;);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;Content-Type: &quot; + JPEG_CONTENT_TYPE);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println();
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(JPEG_CONTENT);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(&quot;--kwkIqb-fsdbtcNpB4dJ_Xqf1-3b0Hp_VF9D0vsgL&quot;);
+
+        reguestInputStreamData.close();
+        this.requestInputStreamData = requestInputStreamData.toByteArray();
+    }
+
+    private void createRequest(String jsonBody) {
+        ByteArrayOutputStream requestInputStreamData = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
+
+        PrintStream reguestInputStreamData = new PrintStream(requestInputStreamData);
+        reguestInputStreamData.println(jsonBody);
+
+        reguestInputStreamData.close();
+        this.requestInputStreamData = requestInputStreamData.toByteArray();
+    }
+
+    private void setUpRequestMock(org.forgerock.http.Request request, String contentType)
+            throws IOException {
+        request.getHeaders().putSingle(ContentTypeHeader.NAME, contentType);
+        request.setEntity(requestInputStreamData);
+    }
+
+    private void testMultiPartResult(JsonValue result) {
+        assertThat(result != null);
+
+        assertThat(result.get(UID).asString() != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(UID).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(ALICE));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY).asString() != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(JPEG_PART_FILENAME));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY).asString() != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(
+                Base64url.encode(JPEG_CONTENT.getBytes())));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY).asString() != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(JPEG_CONTENT_TYPE));
+    }
+
+    private void testNonMultiPartResult(JsonValue result) {
+        assertThat(result != null);
+
+        assertThat(result.get(UID).asString() != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(UID).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(ALICE));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY) != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY).get(&quot;$ref&quot;).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(
+                &quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#filename&quot;));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY) != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY).get(&quot;$ref&quot;).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(
+                &quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#content&quot;));
+
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY) != null);
+        assertThat(result.get(PROFILE_MIMETYPE_KEY).get(&quot;$ref&quot;).asString().equalsIgnoreCase(
+                &quot;cid:&quot; + JPEG_PART_NAME + &quot;#mimetype&quot;));
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void testShouldPopulateReferencesWhenGetJsonActionContentIsCalled()
+            throws ResourceException, IOException {

+                assertThat(operation.getValue().asString().equalsIgnoreCase(JPEG_CONTENT_TYPE));
+            } else if (field.equalsIgnoreCase(PROFILE_CONTENT_KEY)) {
+                assertThat(operation.getValue().asString().equals(
+                        Base64url.encode(JPEG_CONTENT.getBytes())));
+            } else if (field.equalsIgnoreCase(PROFILE_FILENAME_KEY)) {
+                assertThat(operation.getValue().asString().equalsIgnoreCase(JPEG_PART_FILENAME));
+            } else {
+                throw new BadRequestException();
+            }
+        }
+    }

+package org.forgerock.json.resource.http;
+
+import static org.testng.Assert.assertEquals;
+import static org.testng.Assert.assertTrue;
+
+import java.io.IOException;
+import java.io.OutputStream;
+import java.nio.charset.Charset;
+
+import org.forgerock.http.io.BranchingInputStream;
+import org.testng.annotations.Test;
+
+public class PipeBufferedStreamTest {
+
+    @Test
+    public void shouldReReadWritesFromSeparateBranches() throws IOException {
+
+        //Given
+        byte[] firstBytes = (&quot;{\&quot;result\&quot;:[{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;).getBytes(Charset.forName(&quot;UTF-8&quot;));
+        byte[] secondBytes = (&quot;\&quot;error\&quot;:{\&quot;code\&quot;:404,\&quot;reason\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;,\&quot;message\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;}}&quot;)
+                .getBytes(Charset.forName(&quot;UTF-8&quot;));
+
+        PipeBufferedStream pipe = new PipeBufferedStream();
+        OutputStream outputStream = pipe.getIn();
+        BranchingInputStream inputStream = pipe.getOut();
+        BranchingInputStream branch = inputStream.branch();
+
+        //When
+        for (byte i : firstBytes) {
+            outputStream.write(i);
+        }
+        byte[] firstRead = new byte[firstBytes.length];
+
+        inputStream.read(firstRead);
+
+        for (byte i : secondBytes) {
+            outputStream.write(i);
+        }
+        byte[] secondRead = new byte[firstBytes.length + secondBytes.length];
+        branch.read(secondRead);
+
+        //Then
+        assertEquals(new String(firstRead), &quot;{\&quot;result\&quot;:[&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot; + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;);
+        assertEquals(new String(secondRead), &quot;{\&quot;result\&quot;:[&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot; + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;error\&quot;:{\&quot;code\&quot;:404,\&quot;reason\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;,\&quot;message\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;}}&quot;);
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void shouldReadSubsequentWrites() throws IOException {
+
+        //Given
+        byte[] firstBytes = (&quot;{\&quot;result\&quot;:[{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;).getBytes(Charset.forName(&quot;UTF-8&quot;));
+        byte[] secondBytes = (&quot;\&quot;error\&quot;:{\&quot;code\&quot;:404,\&quot;reason\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;,\&quot;message\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;}}&quot;)
+                .getBytes(Charset.forName(&quot;UTF-8&quot;));
+
+        PipeBufferedStream pipe = new PipeBufferedStream();
+        OutputStream outputStream = pipe.getIn();
+        BranchingInputStream inputStream = pipe.getOut();
+
+        //When
+        for (byte i : firstBytes) {
+            outputStream.write(i);
+        }
+        byte[] firstRead = new byte[firstBytes.length];
+        inputStream.read(firstRead);
+
+        //Then input stream should be empty as have read everything from output stream.
+        int empty = inputStream.read();
+        assertTrue(empty == -1);
+
+        for (byte i : secondBytes) {
+            outputStream.write(i);
+        }
+        byte[] secondRead = new byte[secondBytes.length];
+        inputStream.read(secondRead);
+
+        //Then
+        String fullRead = new String(firstRead) + new String(secondRead);
+        assertEquals(fullRead, &quot;{\&quot;result\&quot;:[&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot; + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;error\&quot;:{\&quot;code\&quot;:404,\&quot;reason\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;,\&quot;message\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;}}&quot;);
+    }
+}
