+import org.forgerock.util.promise.Promises;
+import org.mockito.ArgumentCaptor;
+import org.mockito.Matchers;
+import org.testng.annotations.Test;
+
+@SuppressWarnings(&quot;javadoc&quot;)
+public class RequestRunnerTest {
+
+    private static final ResourceException EXCEPTION = ResourceException
+            .getException(ResourceException.NOT_FOUND);
+
+    @Test
+    public void testHandleResultAnonymousQueryResultHandlerInVisitQueryAsync() throws Exception {
+        Response response = new Response();
+        QueryResultHandler resultHandler = getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(response);
+        resultHandler.handleResult(new QueryResult());
+        assertEquals(getResponseContent(response), &quot;{&quot; + &quot;\&quot;result\&quot;:[],&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:0,\&quot;pagedResultsCookie\&quot;:null,\&quot;remainingPagedResults\&quot;:-1&quot;
+                + &quot;}&quot;);
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void testHandleResourceAnonymousQueryResultHandlerInVisitQueryAsync() throws Exception {
+        Response response = new Response();
+        QueryResultHandler resultHandler = getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(response);
+        resultHandler.handleResource(new Resource(&quot;id&quot;, &quot;revision&quot;, new JsonValue(&quot;jsonValue&quot;)));
+        resultHandler.handleResult(new QueryResult());
+        assertEquals(getResponseContent(response), &quot;{&quot; + &quot;\&quot;result\&quot;:[\&quot;jsonValue\&quot;],&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,\&quot;pagedResultsCookie\&quot;:null,\&quot;remainingPagedResults\&quot;:-1&quot;
+                + &quot;}&quot;);
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void testHandleResourceTwoAnonymousQueryResultHandlerInVisitQueryAsync()
+            throws Exception {
+        Response response = new Response();
+        QueryResultHandler resultHandler = getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(response);
+        resultHandler.handleResource(new Resource(&quot;id&quot;, &quot;revision&quot;, json(object(field(&quot;intField&quot;,
+                42), field(&quot;stringField&quot;, &quot;stringValue&quot;)))));
+        resultHandler.handleResource(new Resource(&quot;id&quot;, &quot;revision&quot;, json(object(field(&quot;intField&quot;,
+                43), field(&quot;stringField&quot;, &quot;otherString&quot;)))));
+        resultHandler.handleResult(new QueryResult());
+        assertEquals(getResponseContent(response), &quot;{&quot; + &quot;\&quot;result\&quot;:[&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;},&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:43,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;otherString\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:2,\&quot;pagedResultsCookie\&quot;:null,\&quot;remainingPagedResults\&quot;:-1&quot;
+                + &quot;}&quot;);
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void testHandleErrorAnonymousQueryResultHandlerInVisitQueryAsync() throws Exception {
+        Response response = new Response();
+        QueryResultHandler resultHandler = getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(response);
+        resultHandler.handleError(EXCEPTION);
+        assertEquals(getResponseContent(response), &quot;&quot;);
+    }
+
+    @Test
+    public void testHandleResourceThenErrorAnonymousQueryResultHandlerInVisitQueryAsync()
+            throws Exception {
+        Response response = new Response();
+        QueryResultHandler resultHandler = getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(response);
+        resultHandler.handleResource(new Resource(&quot;id&quot;, &quot;revision&quot;, json(object(field(&quot;intField&quot;,
+                42), field(&quot;stringField&quot;, &quot;stringValue&quot;)))));
+        resultHandler.handleError(EXCEPTION);
+        assertEquals(getResponseContent(response), &quot;{&quot; + &quot;\&quot;result\&quot;:[&quot;
+                + &quot;{\&quot;intField\&quot;:42,\&quot;stringField\&quot;:\&quot;stringValue\&quot;}&quot; + &quot;],&quot; + &quot;\&quot;resultCount\&quot;:1,&quot;
+                + &quot;\&quot;error\&quot;:{\&quot;code\&quot;:404,\&quot;reason\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;,\&quot;message\&quot;:\&quot;Not Found\&quot;}&quot;
+                + &quot;}&quot;);
+    }
+
+    private String getResponseContent(Response response) throws IOException {
+        ByteArrayOutputStream outputStream = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
+        response.getEntity().copyDecodedContentTo(outputStream);
+        return new String(outputStream.toByteArray());
+    }
+
+    private QueryResultHandler getAnonymousQueryResultHandler(Response httpResponse) throws Exception {
+        // mock everything
+        Context context = mock(Context.class);
+        QueryRequest request = Requests.newQueryRequest(&quot;&quot;);
+        org.forgerock.http.Request httpRequest = newRequest();
+        Connection connection = mock(Connection.class);
+
+        // set the expectations
+        when(connection.queryAsync(eq(context), eq(request), Matchers.&lt;QueryResultHandler&gt;anyObject()))
+                .thenReturn(Promises.&lt;QueryResult, ResourceException&gt;newSuccessfulPromise(null));
+
+        // run the code to access the anonymous class
+        RequestRunner requestRunner = new RequestRunner(context, request, httpRequest, httpResponse);
+        requestRunner.handleResult(connection);
+
+        // Retrieve the anonymous class (phewww!)
+        ArgumentCaptor&lt;QueryResultHandler&gt; arg = ArgumentCaptor.forClass(QueryResultHandler.class);
+        verify(connection).queryAsync(eq(context), eq(request), arg.capture());
+        return arg.getValue();
+    }
+}
</ins></span></pre></div>

-/**
- * HTTP adapter from HTTP calls to JSON resource calls. This class can be
- * used in any {@link org.forgerock.http.Handler}, just create a new instance and override the handle(Context, Request)
- * method in your HTTP Handler to delegate all those calls to this class's handle(Context, Request)
- * method.
- * &lt;p&gt;
- * For example:
- *
- * &lt;pre&gt;
- * public class TestHandler extends org.forgerock.http.Handler {
- *     private final  HttpAdapter adapter;
- *
- *     public TestHandler() {
- *         RequestHandler handler = xxx;
- *         ConnectionFactory connectionFactory =
- *                 Resources.newInternalConnectionFactory(handler);
- *         adapter = new HttpAdapter(connectionFactory);
- *     }
- *
- *     protected Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; handler(Context context,
- *                 org.forgerock.http.Request req)
- *             throws ResponseException {
- *         return adapter.handle(context, req);
- *     }
- * }
- * &lt;/pre&gt;
- *
- * Note that this adapter does not provide implementations for the HTTP HEAD,
- * OPTIONS, or TRACE methods. A simpler approach is to use the
- * {@link CrestHandler} class contained within this package to build HTTP
- * Handlers since it provides support for these HTTP methods.
- */
-public final class HttpAdapter implements Handler {
-
-    private static final String FIELDS_DELIMITER = &quot;,&quot;;
-    private static final String SORT_KEYS_DELIMITER = &quot;,&quot;;
-
-    private final ConnectionFactory connectionFactory;
-    private final HttpContextFactory contextFactory;
-
-    /**
-     * Creates a new HTTP adapter with the provided connection factory and a
-     * context factory the {@link SecurityContextFactory}.
-     *
-     * @param connectionFactory
-     *            The connection factory.
-     */
-    public HttpAdapter(ConnectionFactory connectionFactory) {
-        this(connectionFactory, (HttpContextFactory) null);
-    }
-
-    /**
-     * Creates a new HTTP adapter with the provided connection factory and
-     * parent request context.
-     *

-/**
- * An HTTP context factory which will create a {@link SecurityContext} whose
- * authentication ID and authorization ID are taken from attributes contained
- * in the HTTP request.
- * &lt;p&gt;
- * This class provides integration with the common authentication framework and
- * is intended to work as follows:
- * &lt;ol&gt;
- * &lt;li&gt;An incoming HTTP request is first intercepted by a HTTP filter
- * responsible for authenticating the request.
- * &lt;li&gt;If authentication is successful, the authentication filter determines the
- * set of principals associated with the user which may be required in order to
- * perform authorization. These principals may include the user's unique ID,
- * realm, groups, roles, or LDAP DN, etc.
- * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter constructs a {@code Map&lt;String, Object&gt;}
- * containing the principals keyed on the principal name. &lt;b&gt;NOTE:&lt;/b&gt; various
- * reserved principal names are defined in {@link SecurityContext}.
- * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter stores the authentication ID (the name which
- * the user identified themselves with during authentication) in the HTTP
- * servlet request's {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute.
- * &lt;li&gt;The authentication filter stores the {@code Map} containing the
- * authorization principals in the HTTP servlet request's
- * {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID} attribute.
- * &lt;li&gt;The JSON Resource Handler uses the {@code SecurityContextFactory} to
- * obtain the authentication ID and authorization principals from the HTTP
- * request's attributes.
- * &lt;/ol&gt;
- * The following code illustrates how an authentication HTTP filter can
- * populate the attributes:
- *
- * &lt;pre&gt;
- * public Promise&lt;Response, ResponseException&gt; (Context context, org.forgerock.http.Request request, Handler next) {
- *     // Authenticate the user.
- *     String authcid = getUserName(request);
- *     String password = getPassword(request);
- *
- *     // Add the attributes.
- *     if (checkCredentials(authcid, password)) {
- *         // Obtain principals for authorization.
- *         Map&lt;String, Object&gt; authzid = new HashMap&lt;String, Object&gt;();
- *         authzid.put(AUTHZID_ID, id);
- *         ...
- *
- *         org.forgerock.http.HttpContext httpContext = context.asContext(org.forgerock.http.HttpContext.class);
- *         httpContext.getAttributes().put(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID, authcid);
- *         httpContext.getAttributes().put(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID, authzid);
- *     }
- * }
- * &lt;/pre&gt;
- */

-     * @see SecurityContext#getAuthenticationId()

-    public static final String ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID = &quot;org.forgerock.authentication.context&quot;;

-     * the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute, and the authorization ID will
-     * be obtained from the {@link #ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID} attribute.

-     * {@link ResourceException} will be thrown if they are present but have the
-     * wrong type.

-     * @return A security context initialized using the attributes contained in
-     *         the provided HTTP request.
-     * @throws ResourceException
-     *             If one of the attributes was present but had the wrong type.
-     */
-    public SecurityContext createContext(Context parent) throws ResourceException {
-        HttpContext httpContext = parent.asContext(HttpContext.class);
-        String authcid = getAuthenticationIdAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHCID, httpContext);
-        Map&lt;String, Object&gt; authzid = getAuthorizationIdAttribute(ATTRIBUTE_AUTHZID, httpContext);
-        return new SecurityContext(parent, authcid, authzid);
-    }

-&lt;document xmlns=&quot;http://maven.apache.org/XDOC/2.0&quot; xmlns:xsi=&quot;http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance&quot;
-  xsi:schemaLocation=&quot;http://maven.apache.org/XDOC/2.0 http://maven.apache.org/xsd/xdoc-2.0.xsd&quot;&gt;
-  &lt;properties&gt;
-    &lt;title&gt;About ${project.name}&lt;/title&gt;
-    &lt;author&gt;ForgeRock AS&lt;/author&gt;
-  &lt;/properties&gt;
-    &lt;body&gt;
-        &lt;section name=&quot;About ${project.name}&quot;&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                JSON Resource Servlet provides J2EE 6 Servlet integration and
-                defines a common HTTP based REST API for interacting with JSON
-                Resources.
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                The module provides a standalone &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServlet.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServlet&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
-                implementation as part of its WAR artifact. The Servlet can
-                be deployed and configured with a custom
-                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/ConnectionFactory.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;ConnectionFactory&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
-                and &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServletContextFactory.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServletContextFactory&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.
-                By default the Servlet will use an in memory back-end exposing a
-                &quot;/users&quot; and a &quot;/groups&quot; end-point.
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                In addition, the module provides a JAR artifact which can be
-                used for building more complex JSON Resource Servlets. As well
-                as extending the &lt;tt&gt;HttpServlet&lt;/tt&gt; implementation you can
-                also use the &lt;a href=&quot;apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/servlet/HttpServletAdapter.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;HttpServletAdapter&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
-                which adapts Servlet calls to JSON resource calls. An adapter
-                can be used in any Servlet, just create a new instance and
-                override the &lt;tt&gt;service()&lt;/tt&gt; method in your Servlet to delegate all
-                those calls to the adapter's &lt;tt&gt;service()&lt;/tt&gt; method.
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-        &lt;/section&gt;
-        &lt;section name=&quot;Get ${project.name}&quot;&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                JSON Resource Servlet is built and made available using Maven.
-                Your project can use JSON Resource by declaring the
-                following Maven dependencies:
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;source&gt;&amp;lt;repositories&gt;
-    &amp;lt;repository&gt;
-        &amp;lt;id&gt;forgerock-staging-repository&amp;lt;/id&gt;
-        &amp;lt;name&gt;ForgeRock Release Repository&amp;lt;/name&gt;
-        &amp;lt;url&gt;http://maven.forgerock.org/repo/releases&amp;lt;/url&gt;
-        &amp;lt;snapshots&gt;
-            &amp;lt;enabled&gt;false&amp;lt;/enabled&gt;
-        &amp;lt;/snapshots&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/repository&gt;
-    &amp;lt;repository&gt;
-        &amp;lt;id&gt;forgerock-snapshots-repository&amp;lt;/id&gt;
-        &amp;lt;name&gt;ForgeRock Snapshot Repository&amp;lt;/name&gt;
-        &amp;lt;url&gt;http://maven.forgerock.org/repo/snapshots&amp;lt;/url&gt;
-        &amp;lt;releases&gt;
-            &amp;lt;enabled&gt;false&amp;lt;/enabled&gt;
-        &amp;lt;/releases&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/repository&gt;
-&amp;lt;/repositories&gt;
-
-...
-
-&amp;lt;dependencies&gt;
-    &amp;lt;dependency&gt;
-        &amp;lt;groupId&gt;${project.groupId}&amp;lt;/groupId&gt;
-        &amp;lt;artifactId&gt;json-resource&amp;lt;/artifactId&gt;
-        &amp;lt;version&gt;${project.version}&amp;lt;/version&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/dependency&gt;
-    &amp;lt;dependency&gt;
-        &amp;lt;groupId&gt;${project.groupId}&amp;lt;/groupId&gt;
-        &amp;lt;artifactId&gt;${project.artifactId}&amp;lt;/artifactId&gt;
-        &amp;lt;version&gt;${project.version}&amp;lt;/version&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/dependency&gt;
-&amp;lt;/dependencies&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                See the documentation for
-                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/index.html&quot;&gt;json-resource&lt;/a&gt;
-                for instructions on building your own JSON Resources.
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-        &lt;/section&gt;
-        &lt;section name=&quot;Getting started&quot;&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                The simplest way to get started is to deploy the WAR and
-                configure its &lt;tt&gt;web.xml&lt;/tt&gt; configuration file as needed. By
-                default it has the following key properties:
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;source&gt;&amp;lt;servlet&gt;
-    &amp;lt;servlet-name&gt;Users&amp;lt;/servlet-name&gt;
-    &amp;lt;servlet-class&gt;org.forgerock.json.resource.servlet.HttpServlet&amp;lt;/servlet-class&gt;
-
-    &amp;lt;init-param&gt;
-        &amp;lt;param-name&gt;connection-factory-class&amp;lt;/param-name&gt;
-        &amp;lt;param-value&gt;org.forgerock.json.resource.servlet.MemoryBackendConnectionFactoryProvider&amp;lt;/param-value&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/init-param&gt;
-
-    &amp;lt;init-param&gt;
-        &amp;lt;param-name&gt;uri-template&amp;lt;/param-name&gt;
-        &amp;lt;param-value&gt;&amp;lt;/param-value&gt;
-    &amp;lt;/init-param&gt;
-&amp;lt;/servlet&gt;
-
-&amp;lt;servlet-mapping&gt;
-    &amp;lt;servlet-name&gt;Users&amp;lt;/servlet-name&gt;
-    &amp;lt;url-pattern&gt;/users/*&amp;lt;/url-pattern&gt;
-&amp;lt;/servlet-mapping&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                You can even check out the source code for this Maven module
-                and run the default Servlet directly as follows: 
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;source&gt;mvn jetty:run&lt;/source&gt;
-        &lt;/section&gt;
-        &lt;section name=&quot;Overview of the REST API&quot;&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                JSON Resource Servlet is a library and as such provides a common
-                framework for developing ForgeRock REST APIs. It does not expose
-                any end-points itself, e.g. &lt;tt&gt;users&lt;/tt&gt;, apart from the
-                example Servlet configuration. More specifically, this library
-                defines the types of operations and their parameters, but it
-                is left to the application to define the following:
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;ul&gt;
-                &lt;li&gt;
-                    The end-points - top-level end-points may be defined in the
-                    Servlet configuration using the &lt;tt&gt;servlet-mapping&lt;/tt&gt;
-                    properties, or they may be defined using a
-                    &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/Router.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;Router&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.
-                &lt;/li&gt;
-                &lt;li&gt;
-                    The schema used for resources passed to and from the JSON
-                    Resources. At some point we do expect to define a common
-                    schema for common types of resource, such as users and
-                    groups.
-                &lt;/li&gt;
-                &lt;li&gt;
-                    The set of extended &quot;actions&quot; which may be performed against
-                    a resource. Only the core operations of &quot;create&quot;, &quot;delete&quot;,
-                    &quot;patch&quot;, &quot;query&quot;, &quot;read&quot;, and &quot;update&quot; are specified.
-                &lt;/li&gt;                     
-            &lt;/ul&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                The following sub-sections describe each of the core operations
-                in more detail:
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Creating resources using POST&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    A POST create request should be used when the resource to be
-                    created will have a server provided resource ID (e.g. a
-                    UUID). It may also be used in cases where the resource ID
-                    is client provided, but only as long as the resource ID is
-                    included as a field within the new resource.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    POST create requests should target the resource container
-                    and must include the parameter &lt;tt&gt;_action=create&lt;/tt&gt;.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;POST&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_action=create&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Mandatory parameter which must be equal
-                                to the value &quot;create&quot; indicating that this is a
-                                request to create a new resource.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be created.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was created.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;POST /users?_action=create  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json
-Content-Type: application/json
-Content-Length: ...
-{
-  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
-  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
-}&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Creating resources using PUT&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    A PUT create request should be used when the resource to be
-                    created has a known resource ID. The resource ID is 
-                    specified as part of the target resource name, and may also
-                    be included as a field within the new resource, in which
-                    case the two must be equivalent.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    PUT create requests should target the new resource and
-                    include the HTTP header &lt;tt&gt;If-None-Match: *&lt;/tt&gt;.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;PUT&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be created.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was created.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;PUT /users/1  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json
-Content-Type: application/json
-Content-Length: ...
-If-None-Match: *
-{
-  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
-  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
-}&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Reading resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    To read an existing resource send a GET request targeting
-                    the resource to be read.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;GET&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType=&lt;i&gt;mimeType&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;A string that identifies the media type for the response content.
-                            When this parameter is used only 1 field value may be returned using the &lt;tt&gt;_fields&lt;/tt&gt;
-                            parameter.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was read if the &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType&lt;/tt&gt; parameter
-                            is not used. Otherwise the requested resource field is returned with the content type specified in the
-                                &lt;tt&gt;_mimeType&lt;/tt&gt; parameter&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;GET /users/1  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Querying/listing resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    To search or list the resources contained within a resource
-                    container send a GET request targeting the resource
-                    container and including either a &lt;tt&gt;_queryId&lt;/tt&gt; or
-                    &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter&lt;/tt&gt; parameter.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;GET&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryId=&lt;i&gt;ID&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;A string identifying a server side &quot;stored&quot; query.
-                            This parameter is mandatory if &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter&lt;/tt&gt;
-                            is not specified.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryFilter=&lt;i&gt;FILTER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;A filter expression which will be used to determine
-                            whether or not a resource should be included in the
-                            returned results. The filter format is described in the
-                            Javadoc for the &lt;a
-                            href=&quot;http://commons.forgerock.org/forgerock-rest/json-resource/apidocs/org/forgerock/json/resource/QueryFilter.html&quot;&gt;&lt;tt&gt;QueryFilter&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
-                            class. This parameter is mandatory if
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_queryId&lt;/tt&gt; is not specified.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_sortKeys=&lt;i&gt;[+-]FIELD,...&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;Optional parameter containing a comma separated
-                            list of field references specifying which fields
-                            of the targeted JSON resources should be used as
-                            sort keys. A sort key is a JSON pointer optionally
-                            prefixed with a &quot;+&quot; or &quot;-&quot; character indicating
-                            whether the key is to be sorted in ascending or
-                            descending order. Default is to not sort results.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_pagedResultsCookie=&lt;i&gt;STRING&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Optional opaque cookie which is used by the
-                                server to track its position in the
-                                set of query results. Paged results will be
-                                enabled if and only if the &lt;tt&gt;_pageSize&lt;/tt&gt; is
-                                non-zero.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                The cookie must be not be specified in the
-                                initial query request. Subsequent query
-                                requests must include the cookie returned with
-                                the previous query result
-                                &lt;tt&gt;pagedResultsCookie&lt;/tt&gt; field, until the
-                                server returns a &lt;tt&gt;null&lt;/tt&gt; cookie indicating
-                                that the final page of results has been returned.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Default behavior is to not return paged query
-                                results.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_pagedResultsOffset=&lt;i&gt;INTEGER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Optional parameter specifying the index within
-                                the result set of the first result which should
-                                be returned. Paged results will be enabled if
-                                and only if the page size is non-zero. If the
-                                parameter is not present or a value less than 1
-                                is specified then the page following the last
-                                page returned will be returned. A value equal
-                                to or greater than 1 indicates that a specific
-                                page should be returned starting from the position
-                                specified.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Default behavior is to return the page following the
-                                previous returned page.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_pageSize=&lt;i&gt;INTEGER&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Optional parameter indicating that query results are
-                                returned in pages of the specified size. For all
-                                paged result requests other than the initial
-                                request, a cookie should be provided with the query
-                                request.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Default behavior is to not return paged
-                                query results.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;&lt;i&gt;arg1&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value1&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;arg2&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value2&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;...&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;argn&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;valuen&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;Additional parameters supported by the stored query.
-                            By convention argument names should not begin with
-                            an underscore. It is an error to include additional
-                            parameters if a &lt;tt&gt;_filter&lt;/tt&gt; is specified.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                A JSON object containing the following three fields:
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;ul&gt;
-                                &lt;li&gt;
-                                    &lt;b&gt;results&lt;/b&gt; - an array containing the
-                                    matching resources, or next page of matching
-                                    resources if paged results have been
-                                    requested.
-                                &lt;/li&gt;
-                                &lt;li&gt;
-                                    &lt;b&gt;pagedResultsCookie&lt;/b&gt; - the opaque
-                                    cookie which should be included with the
-                                    next paged results query if paged results
-                                    have been requested, otherwise &lt;tt&gt;null&lt;/tt&gt;. 
-                                &lt;/li&gt;
-                                &lt;li&gt;
-                                    &lt;b&gt;remainingPagedResults&lt;/b&gt; - an estimate
-                                    of the number of remaining paged results, or
-                                    &lt;tt&gt;-1&lt;/tt&gt; if the number is not known, or
-                                    if paged results have not been requested.
-                                &lt;/li&gt;
-                            &lt;/ul&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;GET /users?_queryId=all  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Updating resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    To replace the contents of an existing resource send a PUT
-                    request targeting the new resource and optionally include
-                    the HTTP header &quot;If-Match&quot; specifying the version if
-                    MVCC is needed.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;tt&gt;PUT&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource to be
-                            updated.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was
-                            updated.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;PUT /users/1  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json
-Content-Type: application/json
-Content-Length: ...
-If-Match: &quot;1&quot;
-{
-  &quot;uid&quot; : &quot;alice&quot;,
-  &quot;email&quot; : &quot;alice@example.com&quot;
-}&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Patching resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Patch operations are not yet supported.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Deleting resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    To delete an existing resource send a DELETE request targeting
-                    the resource to be deleted and optionally include
-                    the HTTP header &quot;If-Match&quot; specifying the version if
-                    MVCC is needed.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;DELETE&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;N/A&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The JSON representation of the resource that was deleted.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;DELETE /users/1  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json
-If-Match: &quot;1&quot;&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Performing extended actions against resources&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Some resources may support additional operations which can
-                    performed against them. These operations are performed by
-                    sending a POST request specifying the type of action to be
-                    performed using the &lt;tt&gt;_action&lt;/tt&gt; parameter. The
-                    request may include zero or more implementation specific
-                    parameters.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Note that the action identifier &quot;create&quot; is reserved
-                    exclusively for resource creation.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Method&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;tt&gt;POST&lt;/tt&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;&lt;p&gt;&lt;i&gt;See common parameters&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_action=&lt;i&gt;ID&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;Mandatory parameter which identifying the type of
-                            action to be performed against the resource.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;&lt;i&gt;arg1&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value1&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;arg2&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;value2&lt;/i&gt;&amp;amp;...&amp;amp;&lt;i&gt;argn&lt;/i&gt;=&lt;i&gt;valuen&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;Additional parameters supported by the action. By
-                            convention argument names should not begin with an
-                            underscore.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Content&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The action specified JSON request content if
-                            applicable.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Returns&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;The action specified JSON response content if
-                            applicable.&lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    Example:
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;source&gt;POST /tasks/1?_action=cancel  HTTP/1.1
-Host: example.com
-Accept: application/json&lt;/source&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-            &lt;subsection name=&quot;Common request parameters&quot;&gt;
-                &lt;p&gt;
-                    The following table lists the common HTTP request parameters
-                    which may be used with any type of request.
-                &lt;/p&gt;
-                &lt;table&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Parameter&lt;/th&gt;
-                        &lt;th&gt;Description&lt;/th&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_fields=FIELD,...&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Optional parameter containing a comma separated
-                                list of field references specifying which fields
-                                of the targeted JSON resource should be returned.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Default is to return all fields.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                    &lt;tr&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;tt&gt;_prettyPrint=true|false&lt;/tt&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                        &lt;td&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Optional parameter requesting that the returned
-                                JSON resource content should be formatted to be
-                                more human readable.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                            &lt;p&gt;
-                                Default is false.
-                            &lt;/p&gt;
-                        &lt;/td&gt;
-                    &lt;/tr&gt;
-                &lt;/table&gt;
-            &lt;/subsection&gt;
-        &lt;/section&gt;
-        &lt;section name=&quot;Known Issues&quot;&gt;
-            &lt;p&gt;
-                See the documentation for
-                &lt;a href=&quot;../json-resource/index.html&quot;&gt;json-resource&lt;/a&gt;
-                for a list of known issues.
-            &lt;/p&gt;
-        &lt;/section&gt;
-    &lt;/body&gt;
-&lt;/document&gt;
</del></span></pre></div>
